TITLE      -Capture cross sections and gamma-ray spectra from     2200600100008 
            the interaction of 0.5 to 3.0 MeV neutron with        2200600100009 
            nuclei in the mass range A=63 to 209 .                2200600100010 
AUTHOR     (J.Voignier, S.Joly, G.Grenier)                        2200600100011 
INSTITUTE  (2FR BRC)                                              2200600100012 
FACILITY   (VDG,2FR BRC) 4 MV Van de Graaff generator.            2200600100013 
INC-SOURCE1(P-T)    For energy range 1-3 MeV, resolution +-67 keV 2200600100014 
                    at En=1.1 MeV (neutron energy spread) .       2200600100015 
            Tritium targets of 0.8 to 1.2 mg/cm**2 tritium        2200600100016 
           adsorbed in titanium deposited on gold backing.        2200600100017 
          2(P-LI7)  For energies 0.5 - 0.9 MeV, resolution        2200600100018 
                    +-33 keV (neutron energy spread).             2200600100019 
            Metallic Li evaporated onto thick tantalum backing.   2200600100020 
           Proton beam pulsed at 10 nsec, repetition rate 2.5 MHz,2200600100021 
           bunched to about 1 nsec. Mean current intensity        2200600100022 
           10 microA.                                             2200600100023 
INC-SPECT 1 Neutron energy spread corresponding to 1 mg/cm**2     2200600100024 
            tritium target +- 55.keV at 1 MeV, +-33 keV at 3.MeV. 2200600100025 
          2 Neutron flux with energy spread between 40 and 80 keV.2200600100026 
METHOD     (TOF)  Sample to detector distance 80 cm.              2200600100027 
           (GSPEC)  Prompt gamma ray technique with extrapolation 2200600100028 
            of the pulse height spectrum to zero energy by means  2200600100029 
            of a statistical model calculation .                  2200600100030 
DETECTOR   (NAICR)  NaI scintillator for prompt gammas in anti-   2200600100031 
            Compton and first-escape modes. 7.6cm diameter, 15.2cm2200600100032 
            long NaI scintillator surrounded by an annular NaI    2200600100033 
            crystal.Energy resolution for E-gamma=1.836 MeV was   2200600100034 
            8.5% in anti-Compton mode, 12% in first-escape mode.  2200600100035 
           (LONGC) Two BF3 counters for neutron fluence detection.2200600100036 
MONITOR    (5-B-10(N,A)3-LI-7,,SIG)                               2200600100037 
SAMPLE      50 or 60 mm diameter disks of 1.5 to 16 mm thick.     2200600100038 
            99.9% chemical purity (except Gd).Samples were placed 2200600100039 
            at 0 deg and 6 cm from lithium or tritium target.     2200600100040
